  <h1><span style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative";color:black;mso-color-alt:
  windowtext'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>◊ INTRODUCTION</span><span
  style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative"'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>
  <div align=center>
  <table class=MsoTableGrid border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 width="69%"
   style='width:69.76%;border-collapse:collapse;border:none;mso-border-alt:
   double windowtext 1.5pt;mso-yfti-tbllook:1184;mso-padding-alt:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;
   mso-border-insideh:1.5pt double windowtext;mso-border-insidev:1.5pt double windowtext'>
   <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes;mso-yfti-lastrow:yes;
    page-break-inside:avoid;height:2.0in'>
    <td width=1173 valign=top style='width:879.85pt;border:double windowtext 1.5pt;
    background:#FFF2CC;mso-background-themecolor:accent4;mso-background-themetint:
    51;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:2.0in'>
    <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:
    12.0pt;margin-left:1.0in;line-height:150%'><i><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
    line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black'>&quot;When
    asked about her past, AURA tells you a long and convoluted tale of her life
    from her childhood to her life spent in faraway <span class=SpellE>Kozakura</span>.
    Born from the prestigious <span class=SpellE>Glimmershine</span> family in
    the &quot;enlightened&quot; island nation of <span class=SpellE>Lantan</span>,
    known for their skills in invention and artifice. Aura's talent for
    artifice and creation at a young age coupled with a wide-idea curiosity of
    the world beyond her home led her to travel to distant lands looking to
    advance her knowledge of cultures and exchange knowledge to other, less
    advanced societies.<o:p></o:p></span></i></p>
    <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:
    12.0pt;margin-left:1.0in;line-height:150%'><i><span style='font-size:10.5pt;
    line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black'>While few <span
    class=SpellE>Lantanese</span> venture far from the western side of <span
    class=SpellE>Faerun</span>, Aura is unusually well travelled, having
    ventured to the most distant parts of and even beyond <span class=SpellE>Faerun</span>.
    Among such places, she claims to have taken a temporary residence in
    faraway <span class=SpellE>Kozakura</span>, a nation in the eastern land of
    Kara-Tur. Aura's talents in creation gave her a place among the locals of
    the village in which she made her new home for three years, after which a
    certain course of events led her to leave on a journey towards the Sword
    Coast.&quot;</span></i><span style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    </td>
   </tr>
  </table>
  </div>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;margin-right:1.0in;
  mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;margin-left:1.0in;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;margin-right:1.0in;
  mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;margin-left:1.0in;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black'>Aura <span class=SpellE>Glimmershine</span>
  is a young lawful good-aligned gnome artificer and inventor from the island
  nation of <span class=SpellE>Lantan</span>. She is kind and idealistic at
  heart, and while she can be rather shy and socially inept when interacting
  with strangers, but easily turns peppy and excitable when the topic strays
  into her fields of expertise. Aura uses the custom artificer thief kit—while
  unsuited for direct combat, it specializes in various forms of utility such
  as traps, alchemy, and a bit of unique magical prowess.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='mso-margin-top-alt:auto;margin-right:1.0in;
  mso-margin-bottom-alt:auto;line-height:150%'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:black'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  <h1><span style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative";color:black;mso-color-alt:
  windowtext'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>◊ INSTALLATION</span><span
  style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative"'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:150%'><i><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Always
  make sure to start a fresh game after installing mods. At the very least, you
  must use a save from before entering <span class=SpellE>Beregost</span>.</span></i><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>To
  install the mod, extract all the contents of the .zip folder into your game
  directory (example: &quot;C:\Program Files (x<span class=GramE>86)\</span>Baldur's
  Gate Enhanced Edition\Data\00766&quot; for Baldur's Gate: Enhanced Edition or
  &quot;C:\Program Files (x86)\Baldur's Gate Siege of <span class=SpellE>Dragonspear</span>\Data\00806&quot;
  for Baldur's Gate with the Siege of <span class=SpellE>Dragonspear</span>
  expansion) and run the Setup-Aura_BG1.exe folder. Follow the instructions to
  complete the install.</span><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:150%'><i><u><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Please
  Note: This mod was designed using resources from v2.0+ of Baldur's Gate:
  Enhanced Edition and will not work for older versions (<span class=GramE>e.g.</span>
  v1.3) or vanilla Baldur's Gate.</span></u></i><u><span style='font-family:
  "Calibri",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Aura
  should be compatible with all <span class=SpellE>WeiDU</span> mods for the
  Enhanced Edition, however, mods that affect vanilla spells (<span
  class=GramE>e.g.</span> <i>Spell Revisions</i>) may cause gameplay
  inconsistencies with her abilities (e.g. certain resources using vanilla
  spells instead of SR-modified ones). If there are any errors during
  installation, please contact me at either <span class=SpellE>Beamdog</span>
  Forums: (https://forums.beamdog.com/profile/AionZ)</span><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:150%'><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Make
  sure you are not running the game on which you are installing the mod. If you
  have <span class=SpellE>EEKeeper</span>, make sure it is closed upon
  installing.</span><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <h1><a name="_OVERVIEW"></a><span style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative";
  color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>◊
  OVERVIEW</span><span style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative"'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:
  0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:150%'><b><u><span
  style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:black'>Baldur’s Gate I<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p>
  <p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;
  margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-add-space:auto;
  text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'><span
  style='mso-list:Ignore'>-<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Aura may be found and recruited in <span
  class=SpellE>Beregost</span> (AR3300). She joins at level 1 by default but
  gains up to 32,000 <span class=GramE>experience</span> based on the PC’s
  level when first recruited.</span><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;
  margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:1.0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-add-space:auto;
  text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;color:black'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>-<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:black'>She joins with a small selection of personal items, most notably
  being her unique <span class=SpellE>Sunshooter</span> bow which cannot be
  removed. Although she cannot use other bows, the <span class=SpellE>Sunshooter</span>
  improves with her artificer level and can additionally be configured to
  change its statistics.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
  1.0in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;color:black'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>-<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:#333333'>If the player character is female, she may show hints of
  romantic attraction. While there is no exclusive romance branch for BG1, some
  dialogue will be slightly different.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
  1.0in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;color:black'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>-<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:#333333'>She has one character-related quest encounter upon entering
  Baldur’s Gate city that involves several battles. After a certain battle,
  rest when prompted to begin the final stage of the quest.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
  1.0in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l19 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;color:black'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>-<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
  </span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:#333333'>Additionally, she has <span class=SpellE>crossmod</span>
  content with the following mod NPCs:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
  1.75in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l29 level2 lfo48'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Wingdings;color:#333333'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>§<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  class=SpellE><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>Sirene</span></span><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'> and Drake by <i>The
  Artisan</i><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
  1.75in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l29 level2 lfo48'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Wingdings;color:#333333'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>§<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>Emily, Kale, <span
  class=SpellE>Vienxay</span>, Helga and Recorder by <span class=SpellE><i>Skitia</i></span><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
  1.75in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l29 level2 lfo48'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Wingdings;color:#333333'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>§<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>Littlun, <span
  class=SpellE>Flara</span>, <span class=SpellE>Moidre</span>, Dave and <span
  class=SpellE>Vynd</span> by <i>Glam <span class=SpellE>Vrock</span></i><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
  1.75in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l29 level2 lfo48'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Wingdings;color:#333333'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>§<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  class=SpellE><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>Isra</span></span><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'> by <span
  class=SpellE><i>Rhaella</i></span><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
  1.75in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l29 level2 lfo48'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Wingdings;color:#333333'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>§<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  class=SpellE><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>Verr’Sza</span></span><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'> and White by <i>Lava <span
  class=SpellE>Del’Vortel</span></i><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
  margin-left:1.0in;line-height:150%'><b><u><span style='font-size:14.0pt;
  line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>Siege of <span
  class=SpellE>Dragonspear</span></span></u></b><u><span style='font-size:14.0pt;
  line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'><o:p></o:p></span></u></p>
  <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;margin-left:
  1.75in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l40 level2 lfo47'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Wingdings;color:#333333'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>§<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>If brought to the end
  of Baldur’s Gate I, Aura will join the party for the starting dungeon. Like
  other party members, she will temporarily leave to be recruited again later.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;margin-left:
  1.75in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l40 level2 lfo47'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Wingdings;color:#333333'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>§<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>She can be encountered
  after leaving Baldur’s Gate. She is found in the Coast Way Forest, close to <span
  class=SpellE>Rasaad</span>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;margin-left:
  1.75in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l40 level2 lfo47'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Wingdings;color:#333333'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>§<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>If kept, her starting
  armor will receive an upgrade upon rejoining.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;margin-left:
  1.75in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l40 level2 lfo47'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Wingdings;color:#333333'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>§<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>If her ‘travelling
  companion’ annoys you, you can force-talk her to disable the overhead
  comments. She will part ways with her companion once you reach a certain
  stage.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;margin-left:
  1.75in;text-indent:-.25in;line-height:150%;mso-list:l40 level2 lfo47'><![if !supportLists]><span
  style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Wingdings;color:#333333'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>§<span
  style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>She has an extensive
  romance path on par with vanilla NPCs that is intended to continue into
  Baldur’s Gate II: Enhanced Edition. More details are given in the
  corresponding section.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <h1><a name="_ARTIFICER_AND_PRIESTESS"></a><span style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative";
  color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>◊
  ARTIFICER AND PRIESTESS KITS</span><span style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative"'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>
  <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;margin-left:
  1.0in;line-height:200%'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:#333333'>Aura uses the custom Artificer thief kit, which is exclusive
  to her.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <div align=center>
  <table class=MsoTableGrid border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 width="69%"
   style='width:69.76%;border-collapse:collapse;border:none;mso-border-alt:
   double windowtext 1.5pt;mso-yfti-tbllook:1184;mso-padding-alt:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;
   mso-border-insideh:1.5pt double windowtext;mso-border-insidev:1.5pt double windowtext'>
   <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes;mso-yfti-lastrow:yes;
    page-break-inside:avoid;height:2.0in'>
    <td width=1173 valign=top style='width:879.85pt;border:double windowtext 1.5pt;
    background:#FFF2CC;mso-background-themecolor:accent4;mso-background-themetint:
    51;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:2.0in'>
    <p style='margin-top:12.0pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;
    margin-left:.5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>ARTIFICER: <span class=SpellE>Lantanese</span> artificers
    are master innovators and craftsmen, making up for their lack of combat or
    cloak-and-dagger skills with expert knowledge in use of arcane runes,
    deadly alchemical <span class=GramE>traps</span> and metal automatons.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>Advantages:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– +20 bonus to Lore.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– +5 additional Lore per level gained.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– +10% bonus to Find Traps, Open Locks and Set Traps.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– May use the Set Alchemical Snare ability once per day in
    addition to the normal Thief's Set Snare. Gains one use at level 1 and an
    additional use every 5 levels thereafter.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>Set Alchemical Snare: Set a trap in the targeted location
    when no hostile creatures are in sight. Traps deal 2d4 (+1d4 extra damage
    per 3 levels) fire, cold, <span class=GramE>acid</span> or electrical
    damage of the artificer's choice in a 10' radius, inflicting additional
    effects that last for 2 rounds + 1 round per 3 levels of the artificer.
    Effects are dependent on the chosen element. Alchemical Snares can only be
    set off by <span class=GramE>enemies, but</span> affect all within its area
    of effect.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>ALCHEMIST'S FIRE: Trap damage increases to d6 and sets
    targets Aflame, dealing an additional 1d4 fire damage per round.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>RAPID FREEZE: Targets become Slowed, suffering a -4 penalty
    to THAC0 and Armor Class.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>ACIDIC COMPOUND: Targets are afflicted with Corrosion,
    suffering a -25% penalty to Physical Resistance and Damage.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>ELECTRIC CHARGE: Targets become Shocked, suffering a 10%
    chance every round to become Paralyzed for 1 round.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– May use the Craft Rune ability once per day.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>CRAFT RUNE: Artificers that have knowledge of magic <span
    class=GramE>are capable of creating</span> and using runes charged with
    arcane energy. When the Craft Rune ability is used, a rune may be chosen
    from a selection that may be expended immediately or imbued on a target to
    discharge under specific triggers to cast a powerful arcane spell.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– May use the Advanced Alchemy ability at will.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>ADVANCED ALCHEMY: <span class=SpellE>Lantanese</span>
    artificers are skilled in chemistry and potion-making. This skill may be
    used to craft <span class=GramE>a number of</span> potions or alchemical
    weapons. The types of potions available for crafting increase with the
    artificer's level.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– May use Analyze at will.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>ANALYZE: With this ability, the user carefully observes the
    target and identifies their strengths and weaknesses, revealing their Hit
    Die, THAC0, Saving Throws, Magic Resistance, Damage <span class=GramE>Resistance</span>
    and vulnerability to Poison and Backstabs. This ability may be used an
    unlimited number of times.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– 3rd level: May use the Infusion ability once per day.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>INFUSION: The artificer infuses their allies' weapons. All
    party members' weapons are treated as having a +1 enchantment for the
    purposes of determining what they can hit for 8 hours. This ability can
    only be used outside of combat.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– 8th level: Infusion's enchantment bonus increases to +2.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– 9th level: May use the Craft Automaton ability once per
    day.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>CRAFT AUTOMATON: The artificer spends two rounds to
    assimilate a powerful automaton which can be controlled at will. Automatons
    last until destroyed, are disabled if their creator is incapacitated, lose
    control if their creator's mind is affected and fall apart if their creator
    is killed. Only one automaton can be controlled at any given time.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– 10th level: Gains an additional use of Craft Rune.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– 16th level: Infusion's enchantment bonus increases to +3.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– 18th level: Soul of Artifice: +1 bonus to Saving Throws.
    This bonus increases to +3 while under the effects of Infusion.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– 20th level: Gains an additional use of Craft Rune.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– 24th level: Infusion's enchantment bonus increases to +4.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– 32nd level: Infusion's enchantment bonus increases to +5.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– 40th level: Infusion's enchantment bonus increases to +6.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>Disadvantages:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– Hit Die: d4<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– Base THAC0 progresses as a Mage of the same level.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– -10% penalty to Pick Pockets, Hide in Shadows and Move
    Silently.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
    .5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– No backstab multiplier.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
    margin-left:.5in'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'>– May only distribute 20 skill points per level among
    thieving skills.</span><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    </td>
   </tr>
  </table>
  </div>
  <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:0in;margin-left:
  1.0in'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:
  1.0in;line-height:150%'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:#333333'>Aura can also optionally be installed as a multi-classed
  Illusionist / Artificer (note: Installing mods that expand upon mage kits for
  gnomes will cause her class to display as a regular Mage / Artificer in the
  character records!) or as a Priestess / Artificer. The Priestess is a custom
  cleric kit designed for thematic purposes:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <div align=center>
  <table class=MsoTableGrid border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 width="69%"
   style='width:69.76%;border-collapse:collapse;border:none;mso-border-alt:
   double windowtext 1.5pt;mso-yfti-tbllook:1184;mso-padding-alt:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;
   mso-border-insideh:1.5pt double windowtext;mso-border-insidev:1.5pt double windowtext'>
   <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes;mso-yfti-lastrow:yes;
    page-break-inside:avoid;height:2.0in'>
    <td width=1173 valign=top style='width:879.85pt;border:double windowtext 1.5pt;
    background:#FFF2CC;mso-background-themecolor:accent4;mso-background-themetint:
    51;padding:0in 5.4pt 0in 5.4pt;height:2.0in'>
    <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;
    margin-left:.5in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>PRIESTESS: Priestesses of
    the Way, a <span class=SpellE>Kozakuran</span> faith, are believers in
    harmony and seek to understand how to manipulate the forces that keep the
    world in balance, gaining powers <span class=GramE>similar to</span> that
    of divine magic in the process. Many dedicate themselves to wandering the
    land for knowledge, tending to sacred shrines, or becoming philosophers.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;
    margin-left:.5in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>Advantages:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;
    margin-left:.5in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>– May use the Spiritual
    Blessing innate ability once per day.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;
    margin-left:.5in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>SPIRITUAL BLESSING: The
    priestess invokes a prayer to heavenly spirits, bestowing a random blessing
    upon the target. There is a 25% chance of gaining +2 THAC0 and +10%
    increased damage, a 25% chance of gaining +2 to Luck and Saving Throws, and
    a 25% chance of gaining +2 to Armor Class and +10% resistance to all
    damage. Regardless of the blessing, the target is also healed for ten hit
    points and cured of all diseases and poisons. However, the fickle nature of
    spirits means there is a 25% chance that no blessing is granted at all.
    From 12th level onwards, Spiritual Blessing is cast in a 15-ft. radius
    around the priestess, affecting all allies.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;
    margin-left:.5in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>– May cast Protection from
    Evil 10' Radius once per day. Gains one use at level 1 and an additional
    use every 10 levels thereafter.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;
    margin-left:.5in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>– From 6th level onwards,
    may cast True Seeing as an innate ability once per day.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;
    margin-left:.5in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>Disadvantages:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;
    margin-left:.5in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>– May only be proficient in
    clubs, <span class=SpellE>quarterstaves</span>, short bows and slings.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;
    margin-left:.5in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>– May not wear armor
    heavier than studded leather.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
    <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;
    margin-left:.5in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
    font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;color:#333333'>– May not be chaotic or
    evil-aligned.</span><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
    color:#333333'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
    </td>
   </tr>
  </table>
  </div>
  <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;margin-left:
  0in;mso-mirror-indents:yes'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:#333333'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  <p style='margin-top:7.5pt;margin-right:1.0in;margin-bottom:7.5pt;margin-left:
  1.0in;line-height:200%'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  color:#333333'>If installed as a multi-class, dialogue may be slightly
  altered in some cases to account for the change, although there are no major
  differences.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <h1><a name="_FRIENDSHIP,_ROMANCE,_AND"></a><span style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative";
  color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>◊
  FRIENDSHIP, ROMANCE, AND OTHER THINGS</span><span style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative"'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;line-height:150%'><b><u><span
  style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Baldur’s Gate I</span></u></b><b><u><span
  style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
  margin-left:1.0in;line-height:200%'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Aura will regularly
  initiate conversation with the player character, first on a timer- and then
  an event-based schedule. The player can learn more about her background and
  other things about her. If you’re not interested, you can force-talk her to
  access Player-Initiated Dialogue to shut her up. This can be undone at any
  time.</span><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
  margin-left:1.0in;line-height:200%'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Player-Initiated Dialogue
  also allows you to learn other bits of lore, with more content being added
  the further along you are in her friendship path. You may also flirt with her
  if you are a female player character to get different responses, but there is
  no romance-exclusive content in Baldur’s Gate I.</span><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
  margin-left:1.0in;line-height:200%'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>As an artificer, Aura may
  be able to modify certain magical items you acquire throughout your journey.
  She will automatically speak up after a certain amount of time has passed
  once acquiring a modifiable item, and you may allow her to work on it
  whenever you please. This process takes a variable amount of in-game time
  depending on the item being modified. Bear in mind that Aura’s modifications
  do not simply make the items <i>better</i> but <i>different</i>, and you may
  prefer a specific item to remain the way it is.</span><span style='font-family:
  "Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;line-height:150%'><b><u><span
  style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Siege of <span
  class=SpellE>Dragonspear</span></span></u></b><span style='font-size:14.0pt;
  line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
  margin-left:1.0in;line-height:200%'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>As in Baldur’s Gate I, Aura
  will regularly converse with the player character. If you are a female with
  12+ Intelligence and 10+ Charisma, she can be romanced, which extends certain
  dialogues in the friendship path and adds a few new dialogues near the
  endgame.</span><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;
  margin-left:1.0in;line-height:200%'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Aura does not modify any
  items in Siege of <span class=SpellE>Dragonspear</span>, owing to being too
  occupied with war efforts. However, she does introduce a couple of new items
  to the player during certain parts of the plot. This is available regardless
  of <span class=GramE>whether or not</span> she is in the party.</span><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:1.0in;line-height:200%'><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:black;
  mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Aura also introduces an alternative solution to the
  ‘poisoning’ subplot during the latter half of Siege of <span class=SpellE>Dragonspear</span>.
  Again, her presence in the party is not required.</span><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <h1><a name="_FREQUENTLY_ASKED_QUESTIONS"></a><span style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative";
  color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>◊
  FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS</span><span style='font-family:"Cinzel Decorative"'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5in;line-height:150%'><b><u><span
  style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Baldur’s Gate I</span></u></b><b><u><span
  style='font-size:14.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:1.0in'><b><span style='font-family:
  "Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Q:</span></b><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:black;
  mso-color-alt:windowtext'> Where can I find Aura in Baldur’s Gate I?</span><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:1.0in'><b><span style='font-family:
  "Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>A:
  </span></b><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;
  color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>In case you missed it, she’s in <span
  class=SpellE>Beregost</span>. Specifically, in the town square next to the
  monument.</span><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:1.0in'><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
  mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:
  minor-latin'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:1.0in'><b><span style='font-family:
  "Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Q:</span></b><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:black;
  mso-color-alt:windowtext'> Will she join my evil protagonist?</span><span
  style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
  mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:1.0in'><b><span style='font-family:
  "Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>A:
  </span></b><span style='font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
  minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-latin;
  color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext'>Yes, <span class=GramE>as long as</span>
  you’re not rude to her, she’ll be happy to join you regardless of alignment.
  However, should your reputation drop too low, you may be in for a nasty
